GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v - c0*beta*v - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine if any candidate can match it.

**GT numerical expression:**
`-0.748*v*(1 - x²) - 0.378*v*sin(x) - 0.756*v - 3.870*x*exp(-|x|) + 0.265*sin(t)`

Let me expand this:
- `-0.748*v + 0.748*v*x² - 0.378*v*sin(x) - 0.756*v - 3.870*x*exp(-|x|) + 0.265*sin(t)`
- `= 0.748*v*x² - 0.378*v*sin(x) - 1.504*v - 3.870*x*exp(-|x|) + 0.265*sin(t)`

The GT contains these structural components:
1. `v*x²` term
2. `v*sin(x)` term
3. `v` term (linear)
4. `x*exp(-|x|)` term
5. `sin(t)` term

Key observations: The GT has `sin(t)`, `sin(x)`, and `x*exp(-|x|)` terms. None of the polynomial-based candidates can exactly reproduce `sin(t)`, `sin(x)`, or `x*exp(-|x|)`.

Let me check candidates with `cos(t)` or `sin(t)` terms - candidates 1, 5, 13, 17, 32 have `cos(t)` terms. But `cos(t) ≠ sin(t)` in general (though `cos(t - π/2) = sin(t)`). Candidates with `cos(c*t + ...)` could match `sin(t)` by phase shift.

But even if we handle `sin(t)`, we still need `sin(x)` and `x*exp(-|x|)`. No candidate has both.

The term `x*exp(-|x|)` is very specific. No candidate has `exp(-|x|)` or `x*exp(-|x|)`. The `exp(c*x)` terms in candidates are smooth exponentials, not `exp(-|x|)`.

Similarly, `v*sin(x)` appears in the GT but no candidate has `sin(x)` multiplied by `v`.

The question is whether any candidate can **exactly** match the GT for all values of x, t, v. Given the structural mismatch (no `x*exp(-|x|)`, no `v*sin(x)`, no `sin(t)` in most candidates), none can be exactly equivalent.

Let me double-check candidates with `tanh` and `cos` (like 2, 7, 8, 26, 32, 45) - these have nonlinear functions but:
- `tanh` cannot reproduce `x*exp(-|x|)` exactly
- `cos(c4*x + c5*v)` mixes x and v in a way that can't separate into `v*sin(x)` terms

Candidate 32: `c0*tanh(c1*x + c2) + c3*cos(c4*x + c5*v) + c6*v²*exp(c7*x) + c8*cos(c9*t)`
- `cos(c9*t)` can give `sin(t)` with phase shift? No, `cos(c9*t)` alone can't become `sin(t)` without a phase shift parameter. It's `cos(c9*t)`, not `cos(c9*t + c10)`.

Actually, looking more carefully at candidate 32: it has `c8*cos(c9*t)` - setting c9=1 gives `cos(t)`, not `sin(t)`. There's no phase parameter for t.

None of the candidates can reproduce all three special functions: `sin(t)`, `v*sin(x)`, and `x*exp(-|x|)` simultaneously.

Even approximately matching structures like `tanh` for `x*exp(-|x|)` won't give exact equivalence.

[NO MATCH]

After careful analysis, none of the candidate formulas can be made mathematically equivalent to the Ground Truth. The GT contains three structurally distinct components—`sin(t)`, `v*sin(x)`, and `x*exp(-|x|)`—that cannot be simultaneously reproduced by any single candidate:

1. No candidate contains `v*sin(x)` or any mechanism to generate it.
2. The `x*exp(-|x|)` term involves a non-smooth absolute value in the exponent, which `exp(c*x)` terms in candidates cannot replicate for all x.
3. Most candidates lack `sin(t)` entirely, and those with `cos(c*t)` lack phase-shift parameters to convert to `sin(t)`.

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (PO43)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v - c0*beta*v - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.748007302808642*v*(1 - x**2) - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 0.755657675270524*v - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

Let me expand this:
- `0.748007302808642*v*x**2 - 0.748007302808642*v - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 0.755657675270524*v - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

Combining v terms:
- `0.748007302808642*v*x**2 - 1.503664978079166*v - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

The GT contains these basis functions:
1. `v*x**2` (linear in v, quadratic in x)
2. `v` (linear)
3. `v*sin(x)` (linear in v, sinusoidal in x)
4. `x*exp(-|x|)` (involves absolute value)
5. `sin(t)` (sinusoidal in t)

This is a very specific combination. Let me check each candidate:

**Key observations about GT basis functions:**
- `v*sin(x)` - requires sin(x) multiplied by v
- `x*exp(-|x|)` - requires exp(-|x|) multiplied by x
- `sin(t)` - requires sinusoidal dependence on t
- `v*x²` and `v` - polynomial in x times v

Now let me systematically check candidates. Most candidates use polynomial terms, `v**2*exp(cx)`, `v**3`, etc. which are fundamentally different from the GT's basis functions. The GT has NO `v**2`, `v**3`, `x**3`, `x**2` (without v), or constant terms (without v).

For a candidate to match, it must:
- Have `sin(t)` or equivalent (like `cos(t + phase)`)
- Have `v*sin(x)` or equivalent
- Have `x*exp(-|x|)` or equivalent
- Have `v*x²` and `v`
- NOT have irreducible extra terms

Let me check candidates with `cos(t)` or `sin(t)`:
- **Candidates 1, 5, 13, 17**: have `x*cos(c*t)` - this is `x*cos(ct)`, not `sin(t)`. Can't match since x multiplies it.
- **Candidate 32**: `c0*tanh(c1*x+c2) + c3*cos(c4*x+c5*v) + c6*v**2*exp(c7*x) + c8*cos(c9*t)` - has `cos(t)` which can match `sin(t)` with phase shift. But `cos(c4*x+c5*v)` mixes x and v nonlinearly, and `v**2*exp(c7*x)` is quadratic in v. The GT needs `v*sin(x)` (linear in v) which `cos(c4*x+c5*v)` cannot provide for all v.

None of the candidates contain `v*sin(x)` explicitly. The term `cos(cx + dv)` expands to `cos(cx)cos(dv) - sin(cx)sin(dv)`, which is nonlinear in v (through cos(dv) and sin(dv)), not linear in v. So this cannot match `v*sin(x)`.

Similarly, `x*exp(-|x|)` requires `|x|` in the exponent. Most candidates have `exp(c*x)` which is NOT equivalent to `exp(-|x|)` since |x| ≠ ±x for all x.

No candidate has both `sin(t)` and `v*sin(x)` and `x*exp(-|x|)`.

After careful analysis, **none of the candidates can match the GT** because:
1. None have `v*sin(x)` as a basis function
2. None have `x*exp(-|x|)` as a basis function
3. Most lack `sin(t)` dependence
